# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

## #1

- Gear: Key Item
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Bauble
- Key Item: Book of names and node addresses by them
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000

## #2

- Gear: Gauntlets
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Hands
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Stat Buffs
    - Luck ✦ = 9
    - Resell Value = x2.5
    - Movement Speed = Lx2
    - Range = Lx1.25
    - Initiative ✦ = Lx1.25
    - Perception = Lx1.25
- Actives:
    - [Fight Me and Sicken](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Fight+Me+and+Sicken)
    - [Poison Fog](https://xeonrapture.com/xr/XRRPG+2.0/Rule+Modules/Webrunning+2.0/Gear+Generation/Gear+Actives#Poison+Fog)
    - You have access to Tiers I-IV of each of your Actives.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Valdan (Cyberpunk)

## #3

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If they hit they can choose to make the enemy stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or they may choose to move the enemy up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Valdan (Cyberpunk)

## #14

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Reposition
    - You may use your Movement tiles to move willing allies on your turn at a 1/4 ratio.
    - You may teleport an ally using your own Movement tiles at a 1/3 ratio.
    - Twice per turn you may swap two allies (teleporting them to where the other was).
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

## #66

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If they hit they can choose to make the enemy stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or they may choose to move the enemy up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000

## #203

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If they hit they can choose to make the enemy stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or they may choose to move the enemy up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Ydilikian (Medieval)

## #376

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If they hit they can choose to make the enemy stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or they may choose to move the enemy up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

## #776

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If they hit they can choose to make the enemy stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or they may choose to move the enemy up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Asticarian (Modern)

- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.

## #999

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Legendary
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Color 2: Gray
- Passive: Party Opportunity Attack
    - Up to three times per round when an enemy leaves you or anyone in your party's melee or ranged weapon range they may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +5 Attack Plus and +5 Damage Plus.
    - If they hit they can choose to make the enemy stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or they may choose to move the enemy up to 10 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 10000
- Credit Value: 1000
- Aesthetic: Rtolkan (Steampunk)
